		function redirectToProxy() {
			var url = gigya.utils.URL.addParamsToURL("HacebPP",{
				mode: 'afterLogin'
			});
			window.location.href = url;
		}
		gigya.socialize.addEventHandlers({
			onLogin: function() {
				redirectToProxy();
			}
		});
		
		function authentication() {
			if(sessionStorage.screenloaded == "login"){
				gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({screenSet:'Default-RegistrationLogin', 'startScreen': 'gigya-login-screen', containerID: 'loginScreen', sessionExpiration: '9999999'});
			} else if (sessionStorage.screenloaded == "register") {
				gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({screenSet:'Default-RegistrationLogin', 'startScreen': 'gigya-register-screen', containerID: 'loginScreen', sessionExpiration: '9999999'});
			} else {
				gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({screenSet:'Default-RegistrationLogin', 'startScreen': 'gigya-register-screen', containerID: 'loginScreen', sessionExpiration: '9999999'});
			}
		}
		
		authentication(); 
		
		function onLogout(response) {  
			if ( response.errorCode == 0 ) {
				alert('You are now logged out');
			}
			else {
				alert('Error :' + response.errorMessage);
			}
		}

		});
